//[l
//っていうか、とくに説明がいるほど複雑なゲームじゃないんですヨ〜。だから、ここに書くこともとくにないんですよねぇ。[l

From the Barista[;

#WRITE(RtPtr, $9D7E98)
// 0x805896c
//私は喫茶店を経営しております。まぁ、分かりやすく言うと喫茶店のマスターです。経営のほうは常連さんのおかげで、まずまずといったカンジですね。あ、そうそう、先に言っておきますが、私は犬です。[l
//うちのお客さんは、音楽が好きな方が多いんですよねぇ。とくに、リズムに関して、かなりのこだわりをお持ちの方が来られます。なかには、パーフェクトキャンペーンをいくつも達成されてる方もいらっしゃって、もう ビックリしちゃいますヨ！[l
//まぁ、いつもはこんなカンジで喫茶店のほうを営んでおりますが、実はこれ、仮のすがたなんです。本当の私は… おはずかしい話ですが、犬用のヘッドホンをしながらノリノリで、はしゃぎまわっているんです！やはり、ノリノリなしではやってられないんですよねぇ。こまったものです。ははは。[l
//わりといろいろな所に遊びに出かけたりもしているので、もし見かけたらナデナデして下さいネ〜！[l
//ではまた。[;
I own and operate a Café.[l
Or, to put it simply, I'm the barista.[l
It's going well thanks to the regulars.[l
And, uh, just to let you know now, I'm a dog.[l
Many of my customers love listening to music.[l
A lot of them have especially good rhythm.[l
And a few have even achieved Perfect Campaigns![l
I was pretty surprised to learn that.[l
[l
I may look all professional when I run my Café,[l
but I'll be honest, I'm really putting on a front.[l
See, it's a little embarrassing, but when I'm off the[l
clock, I'm always jamming out with these little[l
dog-sized headphones. What can I say?[l
I need a little flow wherever I go.[l
It's complicated. Heh...[l
I do go out from time to time, so if you happen to[l
run into me... please pet me![l
See you around.[;

// Plucking Letter

#WRITE(RtPtr, $9D7EA4)
// 0x8058960
//毛ぬき投書[;
Plucking Letter[;

#WRITE(RtPtr, $9D7EA8)
// 0x80587c0
//わたしは野菜をつくっているおじさんです。最近、うちの野菜たちにヒゲが生えるんです！とてもブキミだし、これでは売り物にならないんでヒゲをぬくんですが、これがまたキレイにぬけないのです。こまったわたしは気をまぎらわせようと、音楽をききながらノリノリで野菜たちの毛をぬきました。するとなんと！キレイにぬけるのです！しかもなんだか楽しいんです！音楽のチカラってすばらしいですね。みなさんもぜひ野菜の毛をぬいてみてください！[;
I'm an old gentleman who maintains a vegetable[l
farm. So, one day, all my vegetables just started[l
growing hair![l
It was so creepy! I couldn't sell them like that![l
I tried plucking the hairs, but I just couldn't get them[l
all nice and smooth like a vegetable ought to be.[l
Well, to lighten up the mood, I put on some music.[l
Before I knew it, I found myself plucking to the beat.[l
And... I plucked them clean! And it's even a little fun![l
The power of music is really something else![l
You've got to try plucking hairs off of your[l
vegetables![l
I can't recommend it enough![;

Rhythm Haiku Collection[;

#WRITE(RtPtr, $9D7FA8)
// 0x8054f88
//[l
//[linesize=large][size=large][linesize=large]鍛えよう[l
//[linesize=large][size=large][linesize=large][l
//[linealign=center][size=large][linesize=large]誰でも持ってる[l
//[linesize=large][size=large][linesize=large][l
//[linealign=right][size=large][linesize=large]リズム感[l
//[linesize=large][size=large][linesize=large][l
//[linesize=large][size=small][linesize=small]「潜在的なリズム感は、訓練によって成長させることが可能。日々の反復練習が最も効果的」[l
//[l
//[linesize=large][size=large][linesize=large]日常の[l
//[linesize=large][size=large][linesize=large][l
//[linealign=center][size=large][linesize=large]動きはこんなに[l
//[linesize=large][size=large][linesize=large][l
//[linealign=right][size=large][linesize=large]リズミカル[l
//[linesize=large][size=small][linesize=small]「リズム感は日常生活の中で常に感じ、育てると良い。歩き方や歯磨き、料理の時等、リズムを意識して動いてみるべし」[l
//[l
//[linesize=large][size=large][linesize=large]リズム感[l
//[linesize=large][size=large][linesize=large][l
//[linealign=center][size=large][linesize=large]ノリがよければ[l
//[linesize=large][size=large][linesize=large][l
//[linealign=right][size=large][linesize=large]なおクール[l
//[linesize=large][size=large][linesize=large][l
//[linesize=large][size=small][linesize=small]「ただし、リズム感とノリは別モノ。リズムを意識し鍛えながら、同時にノリの良さも身に付けよう」[l
//[l
//[linesize=large][size=large][linesize=large]ブレイクを[l
//[linesize=large][size=large][linesize=large][l
//[linealign=center][size=large][linesize=large]待てないアノ娘は[l
//[linesize=large][size=large][linesize=large][l
//[linealign=right][size=large][linesize=large]ハンパモノ[l
//[linesize=large][size=small][linesize=small]「ブレイクを正確にカウントすることは難しく、つっこみ気味になりがち。落ち着いて待てるかどうかが、かっこよさを大きく左右する」[l
//[l
//[linesize=large][size=large][linesize=large]大人でも[l
//[linesize=large][size=large][linesize=large][l
//[linealign=center][size=large][linesize=large]メキメキ伸びる[l
//[linesize=large][size=large][linesize=large][l
//[linealign=right][size=large][linesize=large]リズム感[l
//[linesize=large][size=large][linesize=large][l
//[linesize=large][size=small][linesize=small]「リズムを意識しようとする心がけで、リズム感は成人してからでも格段に良くなってゆく」[l
//[;
[l
[linealign=left]Let us exercise[l
[linealign=center]something which everyone has,[l
[linealign=right]a sense of rhythm...[l
[l
[linealign=center]"Your sense of rhythm can be developed with[l
practice, especially when it's worked into[l
your daily routine."[l
[l
//
[l
[linealign=left]You can make all your[l
[linealign=center]everyday activities[l
[linealign=right]much more rhythmical[l
[l
[linealign=center]"It's good to feel and improve your sense of rhythm[l
throughout your day, such as while walking,[l
brushing your teeth, cooking, etc...[l
You should always keep rhythm in mind."[l
//
[l
[linealign=left]Your sense of rhythm,[l
[linealign=center]if your flow can be improved,[l
[linealign=right]gets even cooler[l
[l
[linealign=center]"However, a sense of rhythm and good flow are not[l
one and the same. Try to improve you flow while[l
also being mindful of your sense of rhythm."[l
[l
//
[l
[linealign=left]In a break or pause[l
[linealign=center]children who lack patience are[l
[linealign=right]simply too stubborn[l
[l
[linealign=center]"It can be difficult to count accurately during a rest,[l
and it's easy to resume the beat prematurely, but the[l
ability to stay calm and wait affects your[l
flow the most."[l
//
[l
[linealign=left]Even in adults,[l
[linealign=center]something still rapidly grows:[l
[linealign=right]Their sense of rhythm[l
[l
[linealign=center]"From simply being mindful of it, your sense of rhythm[l
can grow exponentially, no matter your age."[l
[;

Understanding Rhythm[;

#WRITE(RtPtr, $9D7F78)
// 0x80560d0
//[linealign=center][size=large][linesize=large][l
//[l
//リズム感 ⊃ ノリ[l
//[l
//リズム感 ≠ ノリ[l
//[linesize=large][size=small][linesize=small][l
//[l
//解説：ノリは、リズム感に含まれる要素の１つであり、リズム感そのものではないのだ。[l
//[linealign=center][size=large][linesize=large][l
//[l
//リズム ≠ リズム感[l
//[l
//[l
//[linesize=large][size=small][linesize=small][l
//解説：リズムは時間を刻むもの、リズム感はノリで表現したり、感じたり、自然にかもし出したりするものなのだ。[l
//[linealign=center][size=medium][linesize=medium][l
//[l
//[l
//グッドなダンサー ≠ ナイスなリズム感[l
//[l
//[linesize=large][size=small][linesize=small][l
//[l
//解説：ダンスの上手な人が、「リズム感が良い」とは限らないのだ。[l
//[;
[linealign=center][size=medium][linesize=medium][l
[l
Sense of rhythm ⊃ Flow[l
[l
Sense of rhythm ≠ Flow[l
[linesize=large][size=small][linesize=small][l
Explanation: Flow is an element included in anyone's[l
sense of rhythm, but not a sense of rhythm itself.[l
[linealign=center][size=medium][linesize=medium][l
[l
[l
[l
Rhythm ≠ Sense of rhythm[l
[l
[l
[linesize=large][size=small][linesize=small]
Explanation: Rhythm is what ticks at a steady pace.[l
A sense of rhythm is how you maintain that pace,[l
expressed naturally by way of flow.[;

[l
